  height 0
  speed 0
  damage 0
  renderstyle Add
  scale 5.50
  Alpha 1.0
  deathsound "Gateway/Hell"
  PROJECTILE
  DamageType "Legendary"
  +NOTIMEFREEZE
  states
  {
  Spawn:
    UBAL B 10 BRIGHT A_SpawnItemEx("TrueLegendaryBombShockwave",0,0,0,10,0,0,0,0,0)
    UBAL BFBFBFBFBFBFBFBFBF 8 bright
    goto Death
  Death:
    UBAL B 4 BRIGHT
    stop
  }
}

ACTOR LegCyberBombTrail : LegCardiBombTrail
{
	States
	{
	Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 //A_SetScale(ScaleX -0.01, ScaleY -0.01)
	UBAL BFBFB 1 Bright A_FadeOut(0.05)
	Loop
	}
}
